<Text>This restaurant specialty is Asian chicken which their meat is more flavorful and tendered. I tried chicken vermicelli and chicken pho and I love them both because of the ginger fish sauce! I'm a big fan of ginger fish sauce and I can't deny that this place nails it. Also, the waiter always asks you if you want fresh or cooked bean sprouts.

The drinks options they have bunch of good drinks, such as Vietnamese coffee, dau xanh la dua, rau ma dau xanh, yoghurt. I would recommend this place for breakfast and quick lunch.< /Text>< Rating>

In my NTBHO, AAA or a similar service is essential. I definitely don't want any member of the family trying to change a tire in the pouring rain at 0300 100 miles away. Add in Triple A's other services such as veregistration, trip planning, integrated insurance and other benefits such as discounts and you have a winner. One morning I went out to drive and ... nothing. Not even a click. I called AAA and in about 20 minutes the tech arrived. A quick test showed the battery was done. The tech went and got me a new battery, installed it, and took the old one away for me. Here in California recycling old car batteries is required. Everyone has always been professional and pleasant. I found the front desk very rude. I went there on Saturday day morning around 11 am to see a dog for adoption either for myself or my family member. I was with my dog and I wasn't sure if I'm allowed to bring my dog inside or not, because I didn't see any sign and it was my first time visiting this place, so I stand outside and asked the front desk "Am I allowed to bring my dog inside?" I didn't even go inside, but the front desk lady talk to me in a really rude way, instead of just simply say yes or no. And I just said ok, I just asked a question and walked away. You don't want to make people's feeling like this simply for just asking question. Another issue with this shelter is they close at 5 pm during Tuesday to Friday. Most of the people don't get off work until 5pm, if they extend their hours to 6pm, it will make a big difference. No matter how much they take care of these beautiful poor animals, at the end of the day someone needs to adopt them, so they should focus on better customer service and extend their hours. What's the point of being open when everyone is at work?< /text>

<Gmap_id>0x8085807ba10463cd:0xc5c2ed05f846b373< /Gmap_id>< text>
I came for a gel manicure and there are def a lot of pro's with this place - it's a really inviting space, comfy recliners to sit in while you're getting pampered, complimentary champagne/tea/cookies, and a ton of different nail colors to choose from.

The basic manicure is $25, and for $7 more you can get the "ultimate" mani for $42. You'll get the standard mani (cut/shape nails, clip cuticles etc) as well as a 10 min hand/arm massage and time in heated mittens that'll leave your hands and forearms amazingly soft.

There is a $20 additional fee for gel, which they let you know up front (always good!)

Solid choice for a mani in the city for sure.</text>

<Rate>4</Rate>< Review>
I've been here a few times already and so far, the experience here has been great. It's easy to get here via BART or MUNI (e.g., just walk down 1st St from Montgomery station). It's in the same building as Local Kitchen, just need to go up the stairs. On one side is the nail salon with comfy-looking chairs. It's well-lit with mostly natural light during the day. On the other side is the spa. It's darker here, with a more relaxing ambiance.

I come here for waxing since they had a deal, 4 brazilians for the price of 3. The only downside of this deal is you need to call to make an appointment, can't book it online yourself, but that's a small thing to deal with. The front desk staff as well as the spa staff and friendly and easy-going, and they're good at what they do. Every time I've gone here they've been a bit behind schedule FYI, but I'm not usually in a major rush so it hasn't been an issue yet.

After reading some of the other reviews, I'm interested in trying out the Groupon deal for massage + mani/pedi, so I'm sure I'll be back soon to try these out and/or some of their other services.< /Review>

<rating>1<//rating><Text>I am very disappointed and angered by the service I received at Floorcraft. I wanted to give my money to a local business and hoped for the expertise and quality I might not get at the big box store across the street. I found a bathroom sink and cabinet I loved. When it came to the faucet, I deferred to the experienced salesperson--she thought the model she happened to have under her desk would work great—not too modern and small enough to clear the medicine cabinet door. I reasoned she had done this many times, and she seemed very knowledgeable. The wrong cabinet was delivered to my house with a drawer I hadn’t ordered. I was told at first that I could cut around the drawer to make room for the plumbing—I refused knowing full well what I had paid for. Eventually they realized they had sent the wrong cabinet and soon corrected the mistake. It took me some time to get the metal plumbing pipes, adaptors, and extensions (I’ve never installed a sink and faucet before.). When I finally turned the faucet on, it became very apparent to me and others that the faucet was too short for the sink. Ones hands are crunched up against the side of the basin to catch the water—clearly this would not work. I had paid $175 for what I hoped would be a faucet that would last my lifetime. I called and talked to the salesperson who sold me the faucet. She said to come down and she’d give me a discount and try to rectify the situation. I took the bus to the store the next day, spotted a better faucet, and paid $96.56— half price. I wasn’t happy, but I felt we had reached a reasonable compromise. However, the next day, after I left a message saying I was ready to come pick it up, she called back and said management balked at the deal she had made, and I would have to pay full price. I refused. They were reneging on our agreement. I couldn’t believe that they were not willing to keep their word, take the loss, and make a loyal customer—The day before, I had picked out samples in their flooring department and talked about stoves and countertops with representatives. They contend I should have known it wouldn’t work before installing it (They can’t return a faucet once installed). I was trusting the word of the salesperson, and it wasn’t until I turned on the water and tried it that my disappointment started to flow. The project was a birthday gift and my high hopes went down the drain. Unless Floorcraft attempts to make amends, I will never step foot in the store again. I will put my refunded money toward the same replacement faucet from Amazon or Home Depot at a price $36.05 cheaper. I’m very disappointed.<//Text></record></dataset><record>

<time>1612741027777<//time><Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
It's nice to have this park in the heart of RSM.

There's a fun playground for little ones, an atrium for concerts and events, a skating rink for recreational games, and in the middle of it all, resides The Bell Tower Regional Community Center where many activities used to be held (pre-pandemic).

I look forward to the day the city can host events at the park again!

Tip: grab a takeout order from one of the nearby restaurants and a picnic blanket and you can have a nice lunch on the lawn surrounded by beautiful trees.< /review>

<username>Diep Nguyen</username><Time>1502072588845< /Time>< Rate>
5< /Rate>
< review>
This laundromat gets 5 stars because of the convenience and the cleanliness. There's a parking lot (it's part of a small shopping area), and lots of washers and dryers. You pay for the machines with their reloadable card. Card's initial cost is $1. You must use cash to load up the card to whatever amount you want. There is an ATM available if you don't have cash handy. This is very convenient for those who hate going to the bank for quarters.

There are also TVs to ease your boredom, along with wifi. Here's a preview of the costs of the front loading washers: Double load $3.25; Triple load $4.25; Maxi load $5.25. There are also Mega and Magnum load. I find that if I have a full hamper (imagine a regular/typical tall mesh laundry basket), I could fit all my clothes in the Maxi load. You also just need one cup of laundry detergent for that.

The ladies that work here are always cleaning the place so it feels very clean. You're also in a nice little shopping area, so I usually walk down the "strip" and buy something to eat while I'm waiting.<//review>
